Category: division
George has 195 oranges and wants to share them equally among 15 friends. How many oranges does each friend get?
Answer: 13
Explanation: 195 ÷ 15 = 13

Answer: 1
Explanation: 4 ÷ 4 = 1

Answer: -4
Explanation: 13 - 17 = -4

Answer: 16
Explanation: 3 + 13 = 16

Answer: 21
Explanation: 12 + 9 = 21

Category: fractions subtraction
Steve has 6/7 of a cookies and gives away 3/6 of the cookies. How much cookies does Steve have left?
Answer: 5/14
Explanation: To subtract fractions, find a common denominator (42). Convert 6/7 to 36/42 and 3/6 to 21/42. Subtract the numerators: 36 - 21 = 15. Simplify 15/42 to 5/14 by dividing both by 3.

Answer: 31
Explanation: 12 + 19 = 31

Category: measurement
Nora has 6 pounds of candies. How many ounces is this equivalent to?
Answer: 96.00
Explanation: 6 pounds × 16.0000 (conversion factor) = 96.00 ounces

Category: time
If Ian can complete 6 baseball cards in 15 minutes, how many can they complete in 1 hour (60 minutes)?
Answer: 24.0
Explanation: (6 items ÷ 15 minutes) × 60 minutes = 24.0 items per hour

Explanation: 10 + 14 = 24

Category: fractions addition
Nora has 5/9 of a candies and finds another 5/8 of the same candies. How much candies does Nora have in total?
Answer: 85/72
Explanation: To add fractions, find a common denominator (72). Convert 5/9 to 40/72 and 5/8 to 45/72. Add the numerators: 40 + 45 = 85. Simplify 85/72 to 85/72 by dividing both by 1.

Answer: -9.00
Explanation: X + 10 = 2 ÷ 2 = 1.00 → X = 1.00 - 10 = -9.00

Answer: 81
Explanation: 3^4 = 3 × 3 × 3 = 81

Charlie has 4/11 of a bananas and finds another 4/8 of the same bananas. How much bananas does Charlie have in total?
Answer: 19/22

Answer: 17
Explanation: 15 + 2 = 17

Category: multiplication
Ian has 8 bags with 3 marbles in each. How many marbles does Ian have in total?
Answer: 24
Explanation: 8 × 3 = 24

Category: subtraction
Mason has 1 marbles. Mason gives away 14 marbles. How many marbles does Mason have left?
Answer: -13
Explanation: 1 - 14 = -13

Category: division
Charlie has 54 cakes and wants to share them equally among 18 friends. How many cakes does each friend get?
Answer: 3
Explanation: 54 ÷ 18 = 3

Category: fractions subtraction
Steve has 7/13 of a books and gives away 5/9 of the books. How much books does Steve have left?
Answer: -2/117
Explanation: To subtract fractions, find a common denominator (117). Convert 7/13 to 63/117 and 5/9 to 65/117. Subtract the numerators: 63 - 65 = -2. Simplify -2/117 to -2/117 by dividing both by 1.

Category: geometry
A sphere has a radius of 2. What is its volume?
Answer: 33.51
Explanation: Volume = (4/3) × π × radius³ ≈ (4/3) × π × 2³ ≈ 33.51

Category: measurement
Ethan has 6 kilometers of bananas. How many miles is this equivalent to?
Answer: 3.70
Explanation: 6 kilometers × 0.6214 (conversion factor) = 3.70 miles

Answer: 8.0
Explanation: (16 items ÷ 120 minutes) × 60 minutes = 8.0 items per hour

Explanation: To add fractions, find a common denominator (70). Convert 7/10 to 49/70 and 2/7 to 20/70. Add the numerators: 49 + 20 = 69. Simplify 69/70 to 69/70 by dividing both by 1.

Explanation: To subtract fractions, find a common denominator (54). Convert 1/6 to 9/54 and 5/9 to 30/54. Subtract the numerators: 9 - 30 = -21. Simplify -21/54 to -7/18 by dividing both by 3.
